    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.framework.core.controller.camera.Default

    local t = {}
    local ReplicatedStorage = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
    game:GetService("UserInputService")
    require(ReplicatedStorage.module.util.lua.util)
    function t.new(p1) --[[ new | Line: 11 | Upvalues: t (copy) ]]
    	return setmetatable({
    		sensitivity = 1,
    		roll = 0,
    		offset = Vector3.new(),
    		limit_look = {
    			direction = CFrame.new(Vector3.new(), Vector3.new(0, 0, -1))
    		}
    	}, t)
    function t.update(p1, p2) --[[ update | Line: 32 ]]
    	local v1 = CFrame.new(p1.simulation.character.instance.head.Position):ToWorldSpace(CFrame.new(0, 0.3, 0) * CFrame.new(p1.offset))
    	p1.rot_y = math.clamp(p1.rot_y, p1.min_roll, p1.max_roll)
    		p1.rot_x = math.clamp(p1.rot_x, p1.max_rot_x.min, p1.max_rot_x.max)
    		p1.min_roll = math.lerp(p1.min_roll, -0.5707963267948966, (math.min(p2, 1)))
    		p1.max_roll = math.lerp(p1.max_roll, 0.7707963267948965, (math.min(p2, 1)))
    		p1.min_roll = math.lerp(p1.min_roll, -1.3707963267948966, (math.min(p2, 1)))
    		p1.max_roll = math.lerp(p1.max_roll, 1.3707963267948966, (math.min(p2, 1)))
    	local v6 = CFrame.Angles(0, p1.rot_x, 0) * CFrame.Angles(p1.rot_y, 0, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -p1.roll)
    		local v7, v8 = v6:ToObjectSpace(p1.limit_look.direction):ToOrientation()
    		if math.abs(v8) > p1.limit_look.distance then
    			if v8 > 0 then
    				p1.rot_x = p1.rot_x - (p1.limit_look.distance - v8)
    				p1.rot_x = p1.rot_x + (p1.limit_look.distance + v8)
    		if math.abs(v7) > p1.limit_look.distance then
    				p1.rot_y = p1.rot_y - (p1.limit_look.distance - v7)
    				p1.rot_y = p1.rot_y + (p1.limit_look.distance + v7)
    		v6 = CFrame.Angles(0, p1.rot_x, 0) * CFrame.Angles(p1.rot_y, 0, 0) * CFrame.Angles(0, 0, -p1.roll)
    	p1.camera_cframe = v1 * v6

    function t.UpdateShake(p1, p2) --[[ UpdateShake | Line: 59 | Upvalues: noise (copy), v1 (copy) ]]
    	local v12 = p1.tick
    	local currentFadeTime = p1.currentFadeTime
    	local v2 = v1(noise(v12, 0) * 0.5, noise(0, v12) * 0.5, noise(v12, v12) * 0.5)
    	if p1.fadeInDuration > 0 and p1.sustain then
    		if currentFadeTime < 1 then
    			currentFadeTime = currentFadeTime + p2 / p1.fadeInDuration
    		elseif p1.fadeOutDuration > 0 then
    			p1.sustain = false
    	if not p1.sustain then
    		currentFadeTime = currentFadeTime - p2 / p1.fadeOutDuration
    	if p1.sustain then
    		p1.tick = v12 + p2 * p1.Roughness * p1.roughMod
    		p1.tick = v12 + p2 * p1.Roughness * p1.roughMod * currentFadeTime
    	p1.currentFadeTime = currentFadeTime
    	return v2 * p1.Magnitude * p1.magnMod * currentFadeTime
    function t.StartFadeOut(p1, p2) --[[ StartFadeOut | Line: 95 ]]

    function t.IsFadingOut(p1) --[[ IsFadingOut | Line: 145 ]]

    function t.IsFadingIn(p1) --[[ IsFadingIn | Line: 150 ]]

    function t.GetState(p1) --[[ GetState | Line: 155 | Upvalues: t (copy) ]]

    	elseif p1:IsFadingOut() then
    		return t.CameraShakeState.FadingOut

    		return t.CameraShakeState.Sustained
    		return t.CameraShakeState.Inactive

    local CanimEasing = require(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):WaitForChild("include"):WaitForChild("RuntimeLib")).import(script, game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"), "include", "node_modules", "@rbxts", "canim", "out").CanimEasing
    return {
    	get_optic_fov = function(p1, p2) --[[ get_optic_fov | Line: 4 | Upvalues: CanimEasing (copy) ]]
    		local aim_fov = p1.runtime_properties.aim_fov
    		local value = p2.user_reflection.client_fov.value
    		local v1 = if p2.user_reflection.camera_reduce_fov_on_non_magnified_optics.value then 30 else 5
    		if p1.magnification_info then
    			return math.lerp(p1.magnification_info.min_fov, p1.magnification_info.max_fov, CanimEasing.quad_in(p1.magnification_info.current_zoom.current))
    		elseif aim_fov == "not_magnified" or (aim_fov == 0 or (aim_fov ~= aim_fov or not aim_fov)) then
    			return value - v1
    			return aim_fov
    }
